name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Business Queen Room
info:Stayed in May 2024
info:Family
info:44 Reviews
rating:4.8
posted:Posted May 11, 2024
msg:I went to Liuzhou for a May Day trip and saw this historic state guesthouse, not the state guest building. Book early and the price is only more than 400 yuan for a pair of breakfasts. That's it.

Take a taxi from the airport, about 30 yuan. There is a huge yard, and parking is not a problem when driving here.

Turn left when you go out and you can enjoy the scenery of Liujiang River. Cross the bridge to the ancient town and the Industrial Museum. The hotel is about ten minutes southwest of the Liuhou Park and Liuzhou Museum. Another ten minutes walk to the Wuxing Road Pedestrian Street and Qingyun Market. Convenient transportation.

There are many names of Chinese and foreign leaders on a big stone at the entrance of the hotel. In addition, there are two pink buildings in the yard, where the leaders have stayed.

The hotel service attitude is very good, and we were given two boxes of snail noodles when we checked in.

The room is in the yard, on the second floor of the administrative building. The room layout is reasonable and the facilities are slightly old. But the service is very detailed, and even boiled water for us in advance.

It's just that we checked in at around nine o'clock in the evening, and there seemed to be no guests in the administrative building at that time. Fortunately, we were traveling together. If I were alone, I might not dare to stay here and would ask to change rooms.

Not recommended Service: I chose this place because I saw that there was an independent exclusive parking lot. As a result, I drove to the bottom of the main building of the hotel, and the waiter did not let me park in various ways, saying that it was reserved for VIP guests. The hotel has already divided the guests into different levels! ! ! The waiter let me go to the back to find a seat by myself. Behind it is the family compound of the Liuzhou Prefectural Committee, and there are too many small electric cars parked. I don‚Äôt know whether they belong to hotel employees or residents of the Prefectural Committee. There is no elevator in the underground garage. You need to drag your luggage up by yourself. There is no service. I didn‚Äôt see a room attendant the whole time.
Not recommended Location: The hotel is on the main road. There is nothing around. You have to walk to the Diwang Building to have a quick meal, and you have to cross several roads with a lot of vehicles. It is very inconvenient! It takes about half an hour to walk to the Five-Star Pedestrian Street. The location is really inconvenient!
Not recommended: This is a state-owned hotel with old facilities. The carpet is old and dirty and uncomfortable. The sofa is even older and people dare not sit on it. The bed is very hard. One of the two pillows is too low and the other two are too high! The only saving grace is that the air conditioner is powerful enough!
Summary: Not recommended!

msg:Pros: The room is really big. There are free snail noodles and longan. The attitude of the service staff is very good and friendly. There are parking spaces. There is a swimming pool.
Disadvantages: You need to stand in the bathtub to take a shower, and the shower cannot be removed. There are only two bottles of 380ml water in the room, which seems stingy (usually two bottles of 500ml are placed). What let me down the most was the breakfast. Because I had a very good dinner at the Green Island restaurant in the hotel the night before, I thought the breakfast would not be too bad. But the breakfast served in the room is in the Xinghe Hall, and there are relatively few varieties. If you like to eat Western food, you only have egg tarts, and the taste is average. There is no snail noodles, and the only delicious one is beef brisket noodles.
Although I mentioned a lot of shortcomings, I still gave it five points. It is not easy to operate an old hotel, and the price of a five-star hotel is not too high.
